***verbintenis.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:verbintenis.html>verbintenis</a> (9196)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">verbintenisse</i>. Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:verbinden.html>verbinden</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-nis</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:verbintenis.html>verbintenis</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:verbintenissen.html>verbintenissen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:verbintenis.html>verbintenisje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">law</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> obligation</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:verbloemen.html>verbloemen</a> (44440)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">ver-</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bloem.html>bloem</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-en</i>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:verbloemen.html>verbloemen</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive<span class="ib-comma">,</span> of a plant</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to blossom again, bear (at least) a second bloom</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to ornate, to cover with flowers</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to veil, soften by euphemistic phrasing</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to excuse, treat apologetically</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to mask, hide (something unpleasant)</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to avoid, suppress, leave unspoken</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to personify</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive<span class="ib-comma">,</span> chemistry</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to effloresce, let crystallize</li></ol>

<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">ver-</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bouwen.html>bouwen</a></i>.
</p>

<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:verbouwen.html>verbouwen</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li>to build into something different, to renovate</li>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*fradailijaną</i>, equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">ver-</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:delen.html>delen</a></i>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">verteilen</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_English" class="extiw" title="w:Old English">Old English</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">fordǣlan</i>.

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:verdienen.html>verdienen</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">farthienon</i>. Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">ver-</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:dienen.html>dienen</a></i>.

***verdiepen.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:verdiepen.html>verdiepen</a> (20442)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">ver-</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:diepen.html>diepen</a></i>, or <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">ver-</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:diep.html>diep</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-en</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:verdiepen.html>verdiepen</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to deepen
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>Het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:kanaal.html>kanaal</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zal.html>zal</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:verdiept.html>verdiept</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:moeten.html>moeten</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:worden.html>worden</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:om.html>om</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:vrachtschepen.html>vrachtschepen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:door.html>door</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:te.html>te</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:kunnen.html>kunnen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:laten.html>laten</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">The canal will have to be <b>deepened</b> to allow cargo ships to pass through.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">reflexive<span class="ib-comma">,</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:verdiepen.html>verdiepen</a> in</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to study more thoroughly, to devote oneself (mentally) to
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ik.html>Ik</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:verdiepte.html>verdiepte</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:mij.html>mij</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:afgelopen.html>afgelopen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:jaren.html>jaren</a> in <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:geschiedenis.html>geschiedenis</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:mijn.html>mijn</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:geboortedorp.html>geboortedorp</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">During the last few years I  <b>devoted myself</b> to studying the history of my native village.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***verdieping.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:verdieping.html>verdieping</a> (2209)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">verdiepinge</i>. Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:verdiepen.html>verdiepen</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-ing</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:verdieping.html>verdieping</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:verdiepingen.html>verdiepingen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:verdieping.html>verdiepinkje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>deepening</li>
<li>floor, storey</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p>In the Dutch-speaking countries, the first floor <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> the floor one level above ground level. The ground floor <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> called <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:begane.html>begane</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:grond.html>grond</a></i>. Until the seventeenth century <i><a href = vnd.unilang:eerste.html>eerste</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:verdieping.html>verdieping</a></i> could mean both “ground floor” and “first floor”.
</p>
